\begin{isamarkuptext}%
We define roots of negative reals such that \isa{root\ n\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ x{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ root\ n\ x}.
  This allows us to omit side conditions from many theorems.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
